Ongoing work has drawm international interest for its wide application and ramifications. 
Florida International University is leading a collaborative of agencies, industry members and university partners in the design of a future National Full-Scale Testing Center that will enhance the ability to study infrastructure resilience via what would be the country;s largest hurricane simulator, capable of generating top hurricane wind speeds and storm surge intrusion conditions.

]]>tag:localist.com,2008:EventInstance_4954188450604325.759384-80.371304Thu, 29 May 2025 12:00:00 -04002025-05-29T12:00:00-04:00https://calendar.fiu.edu/event/language-culture-and-society-in-havana-in-1830-6579Lectures & ConferencesMay 29, 2025: Language, Culture, and Society in Havana in 1830 at GL - Green LibraryDictionaries and encyclopedias from Europe inspired a group of intellectuals in Havana to compile the typical voices of Cuba around 1830. This effort resulted in a vocabulary that remained unpublished for 190 years, until Dr. ChÃ¡vez-Rivera edited and published it in 2021. The original manuscript circulated in the XIX century and was an influence on the island and abroad. The objective of this conference is to identify particularities of that interest in the Spanish language and the inclination for lexicographic activity in Cuba in the years prior to the appearance of Esteban Pichardoâ€™s Diccionario provincial de voces cubanas in 1836. This conference reconstructs the creative and bibliographic environment of that pioneering group in 1830 who had the good sense to work as a team, recognize aspects of Cuban identity, and capture the various voices and phrases used by their contemporaries on the island.

Over the last century, the Congressional Baseball Gameâ€™s popularity has contributed to its evolution into a foundation called Congressional Sports for Charity. As recommended in our Equity Action Initiative, FIU seeks to align with the spirit of this holiday, to make Juneteenth an official day of observance at Florida International University. Additionally, we stand in support of the Student Government Association of Florida. 
The theme for FIU first inaugural Juneteenth celebration is â€œEducate, Celebrate, and Healâ€. Educating, celebrating, and embracing the truths of Juneteenth can serve to expand the collective knowledge of our entire FIU community and accelerate an appreciation for the Black history excluded from pedagogy, that may have framed a different America. Celebrating Juneteenth complements the work of the Founding Fathers, being the architects of the Declaration of Independence, and brings to the conversation, the 400 years Blacks have tried to achieve equality in enjoying â€˜life, liberty and the pursuit of happinessâ€™. During this week of observance, we will provide programming and activities to commemorate Juneteenth beginning June 14 and culminating with a Juneteenth Freedom Day Celebration on Saturday, June 19 from 10am to 4pm. To learn more about this celebration, visit <https://ace.fiu.edu/juneteenth/>

This unique approach invites deeper reflection on migration, resilience, and the power of storytelling in the Haitian experience.

<title>May 16, 2025: Infrastructure Week at FIU in DC</title>
<description>
<![CDATA[ <p>The State of Florida has recognized FIU as the University of Distinction in Environment Resilience. Ongoing work has drawm international interest for its wide application and ramifications. </p> <p>Florida International University is leading a collaborative of agencies, industry members and university partners in the design of a future National Full-Scale Testing Center that will enhance the ability to study infrastructure resilience via what would be the country;s largest hurricane simulator, capable of generating top hurricane wind speeds and storm surge intrusion conditions. </p> <p>Join us in learning more about out infrastructure resilience through our ClimateReady Tech Hub, Robotics and Autonomy Center for Environmental Restorations, 3-D Printing of Ultra-High-Performance Concrete, and more!</p> <p><a href="https://calendar.fiu.edu/event/infrastructure-week-9577">View on site</a> | <a href="mailto:?subject=I+found+an+interesting+event%3A+Infrastructure+Week&amp;body=I+found+an+interesting+event+you+may+like%3A%0A%0A%0ADate%3A+May+16%2C+2025%0A%0ADescription%3A%0AThe+State+of+Florida+has+recognized+FIU+as+the+University+of+Distinction+in+Environment+Resilience.+Ongoing+work+has+drawm+international+interest+for+its+wide+application+and+ramifications.+%0A%0AFlorida+International+University+is+leading+a+collaborative+of+agencies%2C+industry+members+and+university+partners+in+the+design+of+a+future+National+Full-Scale+Testing+Center+that+will+enhance+the+ability+to+study+infrastructure+resilience+via+what+would+be+the+country%3Bs+largest+hurricane+simulator%2C+capable+of+generating+top+hurricane+wind+speeds+and+storm+surge+intrusion+conditions.+%0A%0AJoin+us+in+learning+more+about+out+infrastructure+resilience+through+our+ClimateReady+Tech+Hub%2C+Robotics+and+Autonomy+Center+for+Environmental+Restorations%2C+3-D+Printing+of+Ultra-High-Performance+Concrete%2C+and+more%21%0A%0Ahttps%3A%2F%2Fcalendar.fiu.edu%2Fevent%2Finfrastructure-week-9577%0A">Email this event</a></p> ]]>

<title>May 21, 2025: Cubaâ€™s Eternal Night at RDB - Rafael Diaz-Balart Law Building</title>
<description>
<![CDATA[ <p>What has become of Cuba since the historic protests of July 11, 2021â€”and the regimeâ€™s swift and brutal crackdown? Cubaâ€™s Eternal Night follows 5 Cubans over 2 harrowing years as they struggle with government repression, scarcity of food and medicine, and the biggest mass exodus the island has ever experienced. Yet amidst the darkness, these five individuals choose to share their lives, boldly and on camera, offering a rare and intimate look inside a nation unraveling. <br /> <br />Jordan Allott is a documentary filmmaker and founder of In Altum Productions (IAP). His work explores themes ranging from international human rights and American politics to Catholic spirituality. <br /> <br />Yoe SuÃ¡rez is an award-winning journalist and writer. He was an independent journalist in Cuba during the filming and became the filmÂ´s field producer. <title>May 29, 2025: Language, Culture and Society in Havana in 1830 at GL - Green Library</title>
<description>
<![CDATA[ <p>The objective of this conference is to identify particularities of that interest in the Spanish language and the inclination for lexicographic activity in Cuba in the years before the appearance of Esteban Pichardoâ€™s Diccionario provincial de voces cubanas in 1836. This conference reconstructs the creative and bibliographic environment of that pioneering group in 1830, who had the good sense to work as a team, recognize aspects of Cuban identity, and capture the various voices and phrases used by their contemporaries on the island.</p> <p>GUEST SPEAKER: Dr. Armando ChÃ¡vez-Rivera. <item>
<title>May 29, 2025: Language, Culture, and Society in Havana in 1830 at GL - Green Library</title>
<description>
<![CDATA[ <p>Dictionaries and encyclopedias from Europe inspired a group of intellectuals in Havana to compile the typical voices of Cuba around 1830. This effort resulted in a vocabulary that remained unpublished for 190 years, until Dr. ChÃ¡vez-Rivera edited and published it in 2021. The original manuscript circulated in the XIX century and was an influence on the island and abroad. The objective of this conference is to identify particularities of that interest in the Spanish language and the inclination for lexicographic activity in Cuba in the years prior to the appearance of Esteban Pichardoâ€™s Diccionario provincial de voces cubanas in 1836. This conference reconstructs the creative and bibliographic environment of that pioneering group in 1830 who had the good sense to work as a team, recognize aspects of Cuban identity, and capture the various voices and phrases used by their contemporaries on the island. </p> <p> </p> <p>GUEST SPEAKER: Dr. Armando ChÃ¡vez-Rivera. Associate Professor and Director of the Spanish Program at the University of Houston-Victoria, Texas, and a Scholar in Residence at the Kluge Center at the Library of Congress. Member of the North American Academy of the Spanish Language.</p> <p> </p> <p>This event is co-sponsored by the Kimberly Green Latin America and Caribbean Center and FIU Libraries. This event is made possible with the support of LACC's Department of Education Title VI Grant. This event is free and open to the public. This event will be conducted in Spanish. To confirm your in-person attendance, please write <a href="mailto:cri@fiu.edu">cri@fiu.edu</a> or call (305) 348â€“1991.</p> <p><a href="https://calendar.fiu.edu/event/language-culture-and-society-in-havana-in-1830-3028">View on site</a> | <a href="mailto:?subject=I+found+an+interesting+event%3A+Language%2C+Culture%2C+and+Society+in+Havana+in+1830&amp;body=I+found+an+interesting+event+you+may+like%3A%0A%0A%0ADate%3A+May+29%2C+2025%0A%0ADescription%3A%0ADictionaries+and+encyclopedias+from+Europe+inspired+a+group+of+intellectuals+in+Havana+to+compile+the+typical+voices+of+Cuba+around+1830.+This+effort+resulted+in+a+vocabulary+that+remained+unpublished+for+190+years%2C+until+Dr.+Ch%C3%A1vez-Rivera+edited+and+published+it+in+2021.+The+original+manuscript+circulated+in+the+XIX+century+and+was+an+influence+on+the+island+and+abroad.+The+objective+of+this+conference+is+to+identify+particularities+of+that+interest+in+the+Spanish+language+and+the+inclination+for+lexicographic+activity+in+Cuba+in+the+years+prior+to+the+appearance+of+Esteban+Pichardo%E2%80%99s+Diccionario+provincial+de+voces+cubanas+in+1836.+This+conference+reconstructs+the+creative+and+bibliographic+environment+of+that+pioneering+group+in+1830+who+had+the+good+sense+to+work+as+a+team%2C+recognize+aspects+of+Cuban+identity%2C+and+capture+the+various+voices+and+phrases+used+by+their+contemporaries+on+the+island.++%0A%0A+%0A%0AGUEST+SPEAKER%3A+Dr.+Armando+Ch%C3%A1vez-Rivera.+Associate+Professor+and+Director+of+the+Spanish+Program+at+the+University+of+Houston-Victoria%2C+Texas%2C+and+a+Scholar+in+Residence+at+the+Kluge+Center+at+the+Library+of+Congress.+Member+of+the+North+American+Academy+of+the+Spanish+Language.%0A%0A+%0A%0AThis+event+is+co-sponsored+by+the+Kimberly+Green+Latin+America+and+Caribbean+Center+and+FIU+Libraries.+This+event+is+made+possible+with+the+support+of+LACC%27s+Department+of+Education+Title+VI+Grant.+This+event+is+free+and+open+to+the+public.++This+event+will+be+conducted+in+Spanish.+To+confirm+your+in-person+attendance%2C+please+write+cri%40fiu.edu+or+call+%28305%29+348%E2%80%931991.%0A%0Ahttps%3A%2F%2Fcalendar.fiu.edu%2Fevent%2Flanguage-culture-and-society-in-havana-in-1830-3028%0A">Email <title>Jun 3, 2025: CHOW Conference (Capitol Hill Ocean Week) at Ronald Reagan Building</title>
<description>
<![CDATA[ <p>Capitol Hill Ocean Week (CHOW) is the nationâ€™s premier ocean and Great Lakes policy conference hosted by the National Marine Sanctuary Foundation that convenes policymakers, scientists, managers, business leaders, conservationists, educators, students, and members of the public to engage in dialogue and debate on significant issues that impact our ocean and Great Lakes and to propose innovative policies and partnerships to address these issues. For more information, please visit the National Marine Sanctuary Foundation website.</p> <p>Each year, thousands of people who have a stake in the future of our waters and our planet converge at CHOW to hear from the preeminent voicesâ€”and future leadersâ€”in our industry, glimpse the future of marine technology, and meet the policymakers eliciting change on the local, state, national and global levels. The topics discussed at CHOW become the mainstream headlines about our ocean, coasts and Great Lakes, and all are welcome to the dialogue. And we need your voice too.</p> <p><a href="https://calendar.fiu.edu/event/chow-conference-capitol-hill-ocean-week">View on site</a> | <a href="mailto:?subject=I+found+an+interesting+event%3A+CHOW+Conference+%28Capitol+Hill+Ocean+Week%29&amp;body=I+found+an+interesting+event+you+may+like%3A%0A%0A%0ADate%3A+Jun+3%2C+2025%0A%0ADescription%3A%0ACapitol+Hill+Ocean+Week+%28CHOW%29+is+the+nation%E2%80%99s+premier+ocean+and+Great+Lakes+policy+conference+hosted+by+the+National+Marine+Sanctuary+Foundation+that+convenes+policymakers%2C+scientists%2C+managers%2C+business+leaders%2C+conservationists%2C+educators%2C+students%2C+and+members+of+the+public+to+engage+in+dialogue+and+debate+on+significant+issues+that+impact+our+ocean+and+Great+Lakes+and+to+propose+innovative+policies+and+partnerships+to+address+these+issues.+For+more+information%2C+please+visit+the+National+Marine+Sanctuary+Foundation+website.%0A%0AEach+year%2C+thousands+of+people+who+have+a+stake+in+the+future+of+our+waters+and+our+planet+converge+at+CHOW+to+hear+from+the+preeminent+voices%E2%80%94and+future+leaders%E2%80%94in+our+industry%2C+glimpse+the+future+of+marine+technology%2C+and+meet+the+policymakers+eliciting+change+on+the+local%2C+state%2C+national+and+global+levels.+The+topics+discussed+at+CHOW+become+the+mainstream+headlines+about+our+ocean%2C+coasts+and+Great+Lakes%2C+and+all+are+welcome+to+the+dialogue.+And+we+need+your+voice+too.%0A%0Ahttps%3A%2F%2Fcalendar.fiu.edu%2Fevent%2Fchow-conference-capitol-hill-ocean-week%0A">Email this event</a></p> ]]>

<item>
<title>Jun 11, 2025: Congressional Baseball Game at Nationals Park</title>
<description>
<![CDATA[ <p>Since 1909 the Congressional Baseball Game has been an annual bipartisan event beloved by all and enjoyed by thousands. Members of the United States Congress from each party solidify friendships off the floor and on the field. Over the last century, the Congressional Baseball Gameâ€™s popularity has contributed to its evolution into a foundation called Congressional Sports for Charity. Created in 2016, Congressional Sports for Charity provides support to worthy and effective charities serving vulnerable children and families in the Washington DC area as well as scholarships to deserving local youth. These charities include the Boys and Girls Clubs of Greater Washington and the Washington Nationals Philanthropies along with the United States Capitol Police Memorial Fund in gratitude to the brave officers at the Republican practice shooting on June 14, 2017.</p> <p><a href="https://calendar.fiu.edu/event/congressional-baseball-game">View on site</a> | <a href="mailto:?subject=I+found+an+interesting+event%3A+Congressional+Baseball+Game&amp;body=I+found+an+interesting+event+you+may+like%3A%0A%0A%0ADate%3A+Jun+11%2C+2025%0A%0ADescription%3A%0ASince+1909+the+Congressional+Baseball+Game+has+been+an+annual+bipartisan+event+beloved+by+all+and+enjoyed+by+thousands.+Members+of+the+United+States+Congress+from+each+party+solidify+friendships+off+the+floor+and+on+the+field.+Over+the+last+century%2C+the+Congressional+Baseball+Game%E2%80%99s+popularity+has+contributed+to+its+evolution+into+a+foundation+called+Congressional+Sports+for+Charity.+Created+in+2016%2C+Congressional+Sports+for+Charity+provides+support+to+worthy+and+effective+charities+serving+vulnerable+children+and+families+in+the+Washington+DC+area+as+well+as+scholarships+to+deserving+local+youth.+These+charities+include+the+Boys+and+Girls+Clubs+of+Greater+Washington+and+the+Washington+Nationals+Philanthropies+along+with+the+United+States+Capitol+Police+Memorial+Fund+in+gratitude+to+the+brave+officers+at+the+Republican+practice+shooting+on+June+14%2C+2017.%0A%0Ahttps%3A%2F%2Fcalendar.fiu.edu%2Fevent%2Fcongressional-baseball-game%0A">Email this event</a></p> ]]>

<title>Jun 17, 2025: Atlantic Council: 2025 Global Energy Forum at Waldorf Astoria</title>

<![CDATA[ <p>The Atlantic Council Global Energy Forum is the go-to conference for navigating the geopolitics energy.</p> <p>Seizing on the momentum of a new US administration in the White House, we are excited to announce that the ninth Atlantic Council Global Energy Forum will take place on June 17-18, 2025, in Washington, DC, with a focus on Collaboration, Competition, and Security: A new era of leadership shaping the future of the global energy system.</p> <p>Energy underpins every facet of national security, economic growth, and the pursuit of a sustainable future. <item>
<title>Jun 19, 2025: FIU Celebrates Juneteenth</title>
<description>
<![CDATA[ <p>Juneteenth celebrates African American freedom and achievement, while encouraging continuous self-development. As recommended in our Equity Action Initiative, FIU seeks to align with the spirit of this holiday, to make Juneteenth an official day of observance at Florida International University. Additionally, we stand in support of the Student Government Association of Florida.</p> <p>The theme for FIU first inaugural Juneteenth celebration is â€œEducate, Celebrate, and Healâ€. Educating, celebrating, and embracing the truths of Juneteenth can serve to expand the collective knowledge of our entire FIU community and accelerate an appreciation for the Black history excluded from pedagogy, that may have framed a different America. Celebrating Juneteenth complements the work of the Founding Fathers, being the architects of the Declaration of Independence, and brings to the conversation, the 400 years Blacks have tried to achieve equality in enjoying â€˜life, liberty and the pursuit of happinessâ€™. During this week of observance, we will provide programming and activities to commemorate Juneteenth beginning June 14 and culminating with a Juneteenth Freedom Day Celebration on Saturday, June 19 from 10am to 4pm. To learn more about this celebration, visit <a href="https://ace.fiu.edu/juneteenth/">https://ace.fiu.edu/juneteenth/</a></p> <p><a href="https://calendar.fiu.edu/event/fiu_celebrates_juneteenth">View on site</a> | <a href="mailto:?subject=I+found+an+interesting+event%3A+FIU+Celebrates+Juneteenth&amp;body=I+found+an+interesting+event+you+may+like%3A%0A%0A%0ADate%3A+Jun+19%2C+2025%0A%0ADescription%3A%0AJuneteenth+celebrates+African+American+freedom+and+achievement%2C+while+encouraging+continuous+self-development.+As+recommended+in+our+Equity+Action+Initiative%2C+FIU+seeks+to+align+with+the+spirit+of+this+holiday%2C+to+make+Juneteenth+an+official+day+of+observance+at+Florida+International+University.+Additionally%2C+we+stand+in+support+of+the+Student+Government+Association+of+Florida.%0A%0AThe+theme+for+FIU+first+inaugural+Juneteenth+celebration+is+%E2%80%9CEducate%2C+Celebrate%2C+and+Heal%E2%80%9D.+Educating%2C+celebrating%2C+and+embracing+the+truths+of+Juneteenth+can+serve+to+expand+the+collective+knowledge+of+our+entire+FIU+community+and+accelerate+an+appreciation+for+the+Black+history+excluded+from+pedagogy%2C+that+may+have+framed+a+different+America.+Celebrating+Juneteenth+complements+the+work+of+the+Founding+Fathers%2C+being+the+architects+of+the+Declaration+of+Independence%2C+and+brings+to+the+conversation%2C+the+400+years+Blacks+have+tried+to+achieve+equality+in+enjoying+%E2%80%98life%2C+liberty+and+the+pursuit+of+happiness%E2%80%99.+During+this+week+of+observance%2C+we+will+provide+programming+and+activities+to+commemorate+Juneteenth+beginning+June+14+and+culminating+with+a+Juneteenth+Freedom+Day+Celebration+on+Saturday%2C+June+19+from+10am+to+4pm.+To+learn+more+about+this+celebration%2C+visit+https%3A%2F%2Face.fiu.edu%2Fjuneteenth%2F%0A%0Ahttps%3A%2F%2Fcalendar.fiu.edu%2Fevent%2Ffiu_celebrates_juneteenth%0A">Email this event</a></p> ]]>

<title>Jul 11, 2025: Sinema Chat-28th Annual Haitian Summer Institute Lecture Series at SIPA II</title>
<description>
<![CDATA[ <p>Sinema Chat is a curated film screening and interactive conversation exploring Haitian identity, memory, diaspora, and belonging. The program features five award-winning short filmsâ€”Tifi, La Vie, Konpa, Boat People, and Prestigeâ€”that reflect on personal and national histories shaping Haitian communities across generations. Following the screening, a lecture will delve into the lived and cultural experiences that inspired each film. The event concludes with Sinema Chat, a dynamic, audience-driven dialogue where viewers engage directly with the filmmaker in an open, conversational format. This unique approach invites deeper reflection on migration, resilience, and the power of storytelling in the Haitian experience.</p> <p>GUEST SPEAKER: Alâ€™ikens Placher is a filmmaker from Haiti. His films have won various awards and screened at a variety of festivals, including winning an HBO BEST SHORT FILM award, having both a world premiere in competition at TRIBECA FILM FESTIVAL, and an OSCAR-QUALIFIED short film.</p> <p>In Haitian Creole. Part of LACCâ€™s Foreign Languages Across the Curriculum (FLAC) Lecture Series and LACCâ€™s Haitian Studies Program of Excellence. Made possible with support from LACCâ€™s US Department of Education Title VI Grant.</p> <p><a href="https://calendar.fiu.edu/event/sinema-chat-28th-annual-haitian-summer-institute-lecture-series">View on site</a> | <a href="mailto:?subject=I+found+an+interesting+event%3A+Sinema+Chat-28th+Annual+Haitian+Summer+Institute+Lecture+Series&amp;body=I+found+an+interesting+event+you+may+like%3A%0A%0A%0ADate%3A+Jul+11%2C+2025%0A%0ADescription%3A%0ASinema+Chat+is+a+curated+film+screening+and+interactive+conversation+exploring+Haitian+identity%2C+memory%2C+diaspora%2C+and+belonging.+The+program+features+five+award-winning+short+films%E2%80%94Tifi%2C+La+Vie%2C+Konpa%2C+Boat+People%2C+and+Prestige%E2%80%94that+reflect+on+personal+and+national+histories+shaping+Haitian+communities+across+generations.+Following+the+screening%2C+a+lecture+will+delve+into+the+lived+and+cultural+experiences+that+inspired+each+film.+The+event+concludes+with+Sinema+Chat%2C+a+dynamic%2C+audience-driven+dialogue+where+viewers+engage+directly+with+the+filmmaker+in+an+open%2C+conversational+format.+This+unique+approach+invites+deeper+reflection+on+migration%2C+resilience%2C+and+the+power+of+storytelling+in+the+Haitian+experience.%0A%0AGUEST+SPEAKER%3A+Al%E2%80%99ikens+Placher+is+a+filmmaker+from+Haiti.+His+films+have+won+various+awards+and+screened+at+a+variety+of+festivals%2C+including+winning+an+HBO+BEST+SHORT+FILM+award%2C+having+both+a+world+premiere+in+competition+at+TRIBECA+FILM+FESTIVAL%2C+and+an+OSCAR-QUALIFIED+short+film.%0A%0AIn+Haitian+Creole.+Part+of+LACC%E2%80%99s+Foreign+Languages+Across+the+Curriculum+%28FLAC%29+Lecture+Series+and+LACC%E2%80%99s+Haitian+Studies+Program+of+Excellence.+Made+possible+with+support+from+LACC%E2%80%99s+US+Department+of+Education+Title+VI+Grant.%0A%0Ahttps%3A%2F%2Fcalendar.fiu.edu%2Fevent%2Fsinema-chat-28th-annual-haitian-summer-institute-lecture-series%0A">Email this event</a></p> ]]>

<description>
<![CDATA[ <p>Founded by Robert Hacker, Director and Co-Founder of StartUP FIU, Hacker Nation ðŸ‘¨â€ðŸ« is a dynamic learning community ðŸ§  created to further intellectual discussion about all things related to: SCIENCE ðŸ”¬ TECHNOLOGY ðŸ’» ENTREPRENEURSHIP ðŸ› ï¸ and SOCIAL IMPACTðŸŒ</p> <p> </p> <p>ðŸ”¥ Register for HACKER NATION HERE ðŸ”¥</p> <p> </p> <p>Hacker Nation meets every Wednesday from 12 pm to 1:30 pm to discuss a variety of future-facing topics, including:</p> <p>TECHAIINNOVATIONENTREPRENEURSHIPGAME THEORYSUSTAINABILITYCURRENT EVENTSDESIGN THINKINGPHILOSOPHY &amp; so much more!ðŸ”¥ JOIN HACKER NATIONðŸ”¥</p> <p> </p> <p>Who should attend? <br />Any student, researcher, faculty member, innovator, entrepreneur or explorer who wants to challenge their thinking is welcome to join:</p> <p>* All college majors</p> <p>* All levels of expertise</p> <p>* All academic backgrounds</p> <p>Weekly articles</p> <p>Every Monday, we post 3-5 articles that may be the target of our discussion in that week's meeting. <![CDATA[ <p>Founded by Robert Hacker, Director and Co-Founder of StartUP FIU, Hacker Nation ðŸ‘¨â€ðŸ« is a dynamic learning community ðŸ§  created to further intellectual discussion about all things related to: SCIENCE ðŸ”¬ TECHNOLOGY ðŸ’» ENTREPRENEURSHIP ðŸ› ï¸ and SOCIAL IMPACTðŸŒ</p> <p> </p> <p>ðŸ”¥ Register for HACKER NATION HERE ðŸ”¥</p> <p> </p> <p>Hacker Nation meets every Wednesday from 12 pm to 1:30 pm to discuss a variety of future-facing topics, including:</p> <p>TECHAIINNOVATIONENTREPRENEURSHIPGAME THEORYSUSTAINABILITYCURRENT EVENTSDESIGN THINKINGPHILOSOPHY &amp; so much more!ðŸ”¥ JOIN HACKER NATIONðŸ”¥</p> <p> </p> <p>Who should attend? <br />Any student, researcher, faculty member, innovator, entrepreneur or explorer who wants to challenge their thinking is welcome to join:</p> <p>* All college majors</p> <p>* All levels of expertise</p> <p>* All academic backgrounds</p> <p>Weekly articles</p> <p>Every Monday, we post 3-5 articles that may be the target of our discussion in that week's meeting. You can find the articles in our link tree here: <a href="https://linktr.ee/hackernation">https://linktr.ee/hackernation</a></p> <p> </p> <p>For HONORS COLLEGE CREDIT, email Honors College Engagement (<a href="mailto:hcengage@fiu.edu">hcengage@fiu.edu</a>) and include: <br />Full name, email address, Panther ID, date of Hacker Nation attended.</p> <p> </p> <p>ðŸ”Ž Any questions?
